The highest was more than 41 degrees, which was more friendly for children. Adults might think the temperature was not high enough. The breakfast was also very rich. Service:

Room facilities:
The room facilities look a bit old, especially the bathroom facilities, which don't look like a hotel opened in 2020 at all.

Hygiene:
The sanitation is average. The cleaning aunt doesn't wash her hands after wiping the toilet and goes to put towels or something. Anyway, you can't think about the sanitation of the hotel, most of them are like this.

Swimming pool:
The hotel has an open-air swimming pool, a children's water park, and a hot spring. Although it is not big, it is still very fun to take children to play. It's very comfortable to play in the water and soak in a hot spring.

name:M‚Äçr‚Äç_‚Äçm‚Äç1‚Äç2‚Äç3

posted:Posted January 12, 2024
msg:‚≠êThe experience of staying at the DoubleTree by Hilton during this New Year's Day holiday can be summarized as: a very uniqueüå≤Forest Hot Spring Hotel, an unexpectedüéâsurprise experience.

I would also like to thank hotel guest service Dai Shijieüëçüëçüëç for his warm and thoughtful service during the stay‚ù§Ô∏è. He carefully provided hotel service information and surrounding travel guide during check-in (see picture 1), which can still be preserved during the popular holiday. The service standard is amazing.

üëèüëèüëèSaving money review:

‚úÖAdvantages: The facilities are complete and new, the service attitude is good, suitable for health resort bathing, the hot spring experience is good, and it is a good choice to experience a slow life

‚ùéDisadvantages: The geographical location is relatively remote, there is no sea view, there are few takeaway restaurants in surrounding attractions, there is no self-service laundry, so be careful when visiting tourist attractions.

Let‚Äôs briefly evaluate it from the perspectives of üó∫Ô∏èlocation, üõèÔ∏èstay experience, üèäüèª‚ôÇÔ∏èadditional facilities and services:

‚≠êFirst of all, geographical location:
1‚É£Ô∏è Compared with other hotels in Lingshui County (mainly divided into Qingshui Bay, Ocean Park, Xiangshui [R&F] Bay, and Lingshui City), it is unique. It is located in Yingzhou Town, which is administratively located in Lingshui County. The hotel is located near Longmen Ridge. It is geographically far away from the coast and not very far from Qingshui Bay. However, because it is in the mountains, the sea view is no longer visible. It is a relatively unique forest and mountain view hotel (and therefore the price is more affordable). .

2‚É£Ô∏èYou can roughly understand the location of the hotel from Figure 2 and Figure 3. It is between Sanya and Lingshui City, so it is definitely more convenient to choose self-driving for transportation.

3‚É£Ô∏èThe scenic spot is not too far from Haitang Bay, Clear Water Bay, and Nanwan Monkey Island, but it requires driving distance. It is a choice that is more suitable for staying in a hotel rather than visiting scenic spots for special forces.

‚≠êCheck-in experience:
1‚É£Ô∏èThe overall decoration of the hotel is in the style of the Southeast Asian rainforest, a bit like Wallace. Hahahaha. The hotel is surrounded by mountain scenery, forest scenery and some farmland villages. The surrounding area is very quiet and there is no noise (see Figures 4, 5, 6).

2‚É£Ô∏èThe double bed room we booked was unexpectedly upgraded to a suite when we checked in at the front desk. The overall facilities of the hotel are very new. The facilities of the suite are exactly the same as the hotel‚Äôs promotional pictures. It has a balcony and is very spacious and comfortable overall (picture) 10,11), the room supplies are quite satisfactory.
ps: I also discovered that the minibars in hotel rooms and even suites are empty hahaha

3‚É£Ô∏èThe parking space in the hotel is sufficient and parking is convenient. The only thing is that the hotel layout tends to use flat sites, so the overall facilities need to be directly connected by a walking distance. Even though there is an elevator to go upstairs after parking, you still need to take the elevator before walking up. It's a short walk to the lobby, which may be inconvenient if you have a lot of luggage.

‚≠êFacility services:
What surprised me the most was the facilities and services.
1‚É£Ô∏èIn terms of service, as mentioned before, the hotel's guest service is very good, even during popular holidays. Room service has also introduced conveniences such as robot delivery, which is rare among international chains for following the trend (although you can‚Äôt order much takeout here)

2‚É£Ô∏èThe variety of breakfast is also quite rich, and Hainan-style refreshments are also provided. (Figure 9)

3‚É£Ô∏èIn terms of facilities, first of all, as a hot spring hotel, hot spring facilities are definitely indispensable. The hotel's hot spring is an outdoor hot spring, and a separate area is divided into the hotel area as a hot spring area.
The hot spring opening hours are 16:30-22:30. There are a lot of hot spring pools (about 10?). According to the nameplate, there are also natural hot springs. The hot spring area provides free mineral water, hot tea, and ice cream. Available. The hot springs open late, so even if you stay at night, you still have time to fully experience it.

4‚É£Ô∏èAnother special thing is that this DoubleTree by Hilton has an indoor and outdoor double swimming pool that is very rare in Hainan (there is also a separate indoor and outdoor children's playground, and the outdoor is a water park). The two swimming pools are open alternately. The outdoor pool is open from 9 am to 6 pm during the day, and the indoor pool is open from 6 pm to 10 pm. The indoor pool is relatively small, but the advantage is that the water temperature of the indoor constant-temperature pool is more comfortable.

5‚É£Ô∏èIn addition, the hotel gym is open 24 hours a day, and you can enter by swiping your room card.

‚≠êSummary:
üëâIn general, I still enjoyed great value for money when I stayed during the New Year's Day holiday. Perhaps because the location is relatively remote, the booking price is relatively very affordable; the overall hotel setting is brand-new and gorgeous, the service staff are warm and thoughtful, and all the necessary facilities are available It is fully equipped. It would be better if self-service laundry facilities could be added to facilitate the needs of families with children. It is one of the best choices for hotel leisure in Hainan during the holidaysüòéüòéüòé (If you mainly focus on sightseeing, you should consider it carefully)
